	if(strcmp(cmd, "/clear", true) == 0)
	{
	    if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pMember] == 6)
	    {
	    	if(sscanf(params, "d", params[0])) return SendClientMessage(playerid, COLOR_GREY, "Используйте: /clear [id игрока]");
			if(!IsPlayerConnected(params[0])) return SendClientMessage(playerid,COLOR_GREY,"Такого игрока нет");
			if(GetDistanceBetweenPlayers(playerid, params[0]) > 8 || GetPlayerVirtualWorld(playerid) != GetPlayerVirtualWorld(params[0])) return SendClientMessage(playerid, COLOR_GRAD, "Игрок слишком далеко от Вас");
			if(PlayerInfo[params[0]][pWanted] == 0) return SendClientMessage(playerid, COLOR_GRAD1, "Этот игрок не в розыске");
			format(query, sizeof(query), "%s %s[%d] снял розыск с %s[%d]", RankName(playerid), PlayerInfo[playerid][pName],playerid, PlayerInfo[params[0]][pName],params[0]);
			SendMemberMessage(playerid,0xFFD700AA,query);
			format(query, sizeof(query), "%s %s снял с Вас розыск", RankName(playerid), PlayerInfo[playerid][pName]);
			SendClientMessage(params[0],0x0099FFAA,query);
			PlayerInfo[params[0]][pWanted] = 0;
			SetPlayerWantedLevel(params[0], 0);
			return 1;
		}
		return 1;
	}
	if(strcmp(cmd, "/tie", true) == 0)
	{
	    if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pMember] == 10 || PlayerInfo[playerid][pMember] == 11 || PlayerInfo[playerid][pMember] == 12)
		{
 			if(sscanf(params, "d", params[0])) return SendClientMessage(playerid, COLOR_GREY, "Используйте: /tie [id игрока]");
			if(!IsPlayerConnected(params[0])) return SendClientMessage(playerid,COLOR_GREY,"Такого игрока нет");
			if(!IsMafiaCarMe(params[0])) return SendClientMessage(playerid,COLOR_GRAD1, "Этот игрок должен быть в машине мафии");
			if(!IsMafiaCarMe(playerid)) return SendClientMessage(playerid,COLOR_GRAD1, "Вы должны быть в машине мафии");
			if(GetDistanceBetweenPlayers(playerid, params[0]) > 5 || GetPlayerVirtualWorld(playerid) != GetPlayerVirtualWorld(params[0])) return SendClientMessage(playerid, COLOR_GRAD, "Игрок слишком далеко от Вас");
			if(PlayerInfo[giveplayerid][tie] == true) return SendClientMessage(playerid,COLOR_GRAD, "Этот игрок уже связан");
			format(query, sizeof(query), "%s связал руки %s",PlayerInfo[playerid][pName],PlayerInfo[params[0]][pName]);
			StatusMessage(playerid, query,query);
			PlayerInfo[giveplayerid][tie] = true;
			TogglePlayerControllable(params[0], 0);
			SetCameraBehindPlayer(params[0]);
	 	}
		return 1;
	}
	if(strcmp(cmd, "/untie", true) == 0)
	{
		if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pMember] == 6)
		{
			if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pUnit] != 4) return SendClientMessage(playerid,COLOR_GRAD1, "Вы не сотрудник ФБР");
		}
		if(MeMafia(playerid) || PlayerInfo[playerid][pMember] == 6)
		{
   			if(sscanf(params, "d", params[0])) return SendClientMessage(playerid, COLOR_GREY, "Используйте: /untie [id игрока]");
			if(!IsPlayerConnected(params[0])) return SendClientMessage(playerid,COLOR_GREY,"Такого игрока нет");
			if(GetDistanceBetweenPlayers(playerid, params[0]) > 5 || GetPlayerVirtualWorld(playerid) != GetPlayerVirtualWorld(params[0])) return SendClientMessage(playerid, COLOR_GRAD, "Игрок слишком далеко от Вас");
			if(PlayerInfo[params[0]][tie] == false) return SendClientMessage(playerid,COLOR_GRAD, "У этого игрока не связаны руки.");

	{
	    if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pRang] < 9) return SendClientMessage(playerid, COLOR_GREY, "Вам недоступна данная функция");
	    if(sscanf(params, "dc", params[0], params[1])) return SendClientMessage(playerid, COLOR_GREY, "Используйте /rang [id игрока] [+ или -]");
	    if(playerid == params[0]) return SendClientMessage(playerid, COLOR_GREY, "Вы ввели свой id");
		if(params[1] != 43 && params[1] != 45) return SendClientMessage(playerid, COLOR_GREY, "Используйте /rang [id игрока] [+ или -]");
		if(GetDistanceBetweenPlayers(playerid, params[0]) > 3 || GetPlayerVirtualWorld(playerid) != GetPlayerVirtualWorld(params[0])) return SendClientMessage(playerid, COLOR_GRAD, "Игрок слишком далеко от Вас");
		if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pUnit] > 0)
		{
			if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pUnit] != PlayerInfo[params[0]][pUnit]) return SendClientMessage(playerid, COLOR_GRAD, "Этот игрок не из Вашего подразделения");
		}
		if(params[1] == 43)//знак плюс (повышение по должности)
	    {
	        if(PlayerInfo[params[0]][pRang] >= 9) return SendClientMessage(playerid, COLOR_GREY, "Вы не можете повысить игрока более 9 ранга");
			if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pRang] == 9 && PlayerInfo[params[0]][pRang] == 8) return SendClientMessage(playerid, COLOR_GREY, "Вы не можете повысить игрока более 8 ранга");
			PlayerInfo[params[0]][pRang]++;
			format(string, sizeof(string), "Вы повысили ранг игроку %s[%d] до %d (%s)", PlayerInfo[params[0]][pName], params[0], PlayerInfo[params[0]][pRang], RankName(params[0]));
			SendClientMessage(playerid, COLOR_LIGHTBLUE, string);
			format(string, sizeof(string), "Ваш ранг в организации был повышен до %d (%s)", PlayerInfo[params[0]][pRang], RankName(params[0]));
			SendClientMessage(params[0], COLOR_LIGHTBLUE, string);
	    }
	    else if(params[1] == 45)//знак минус (понижение по должности)
	    {
	        if(PlayerInfo[params[0]][pRang] == 1) return SendClientMessage(playerid, COLOR_GREY, "У игрока сейчас 1 ранг, понижение невозможно");
	        if(PlayerInfo[params[0]][pRang] >= 10) return SendClientMessage(playerid, COLOR_GREY, "Вы не можете понизить лидера");
	        PlayerInfo[params[0]][pRang]--;
	        format(string, sizeof(string), "Вы понизили ранг игроку %s[%d] до %d (%s)", PlayerInfo[params[0]][pName], params[0], PlayerInfo[params[0]][pRang], RankName(params[0]));
			SendClientMessage(playerid, COLOR_LIGHTBLUE, string);
			format(string, sizeof(string), "Ваш ранг в организации был понижен до %d (%s)", PlayerInfo[params[0]][pRang], RankName(params[0]));
			SendClientMessage(params[0], COLOR_ORANGE, string);
	    }

	    static const fmt_query[] = "UPDATE `accounts` SET `rang` = '%d' WHERE `id` = '%d'";
		format(query, sizeof(query), fmt_query, PlayerInfo[params[0]][pRang], PlayerInfo[params[0]][pIDacc]);
		mysql_query(dbHandle, query);
		return 1;
	}

	if(strcmp(cmd,"/putammo",true)==0)
	{
		if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pMember] == 8 || PlayerInfo[playerid][pMember] == 10 || PlayerInfo[playerid][pMember] == 11 || PlayerInfo[playerid][pMember] == 12)
		{
			if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pMember] == 10 || PlayerInfo[playerid][pMember] == 11 || PlayerInfo[playerid][pMember] == 12)
			{
				if(!IsMafiaCar(playerid))
				{
					SendClientMessage(playerid,COLOR_GRAD,"Вы должны находиться рядом с машиной");
					return 1;
				}
			}
			if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pMember] == 8)
			{
				if(!IsAmmoMOCar(playerid))
				{
					SendClientMessage(playerid,COLOR_GRAD,"Вы должны находиться рядом с машиной");
					return 1;
				}
			}
			new nearveh = GetNearestVehicle(playerid);
			if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pPatronPlayer] == 0)
			{
				SendClientMessage(playerid,COLOR_GRAD,"У Вас нет ящика с патронами.");
				return 1;
			}
			if(PatrCar[nearveh] >= 5) return SendClientMessage(playerid,COLOR_GRAD1,"Машина заполнена");
			if(PatrCar[nearveh] == 0)
			{
				format(string,sizeof(string),"Загружено ящиков: %d", PatrCar[nearveh]);
				Potri3dtext[nearveh] = Create3DTextLabel(string, 0xFFFF00FF, 0.0, 7.77, 7.77, 30.0,0,1);
				Attach3DTextLabelToVehicle(Potri3dtext[nearveh], nearveh, 0.0, 0.0, 2.0);
				VehInfo[nearveh][pText] = true;
			}
			PatrCar[nearveh] += 1;
			if(PatrCar[nearveh] == 1) AmmoCarInfo[nearveh][One] = PlayerInfo[playerid][pIDAmmo];
			if(PatrCar[nearveh] == 2) AmmoCarInfo[nearveh][Two] = PlayerInfo[playerid][pIDAmmo];
			if(PatrCar[nearveh] == 3) AmmoCarInfo[nearveh][Twi] = PlayerInfo[playerid][pIDAmmo];
			if(PatrCar[nearveh] == 4) AmmoCarInfo[nearveh][Four] = PlayerInfo[playerid][pIDAmmo];
			if(PatrCar[nearveh] == 5) AmmoCarInfo[nearveh][Five] = PlayerInfo[playerid][pIDAmmo];
			ApplyAnimation(playerid,"CARRY","putdwn",4.0,0,1,1,0,0,1130);
			PlayerInfo[playerid][pPatronPlayer] -=1;
			RemovePlayerAttachedObject(playerid, 1);
			format(string,sizeof(string),"Загружено ящиков: %d", PatrCar[nearveh]);
			Update3DTextLabelText(Potri3dtext[nearveh],0xFFFF00FF, string);
		}
		return 1;
	}

			if(PlayerInfo[params[0]][pAllowCar] == caridhouse[playerid])
			{

			else

				format(query, sizeof(query), "%s дал Вам ключи от своего домашнего транспорта",PlayerInfo[playerid][pName]);
				SendClientMessage(params[0], 0x0099FFAA, query);

					StoreMO[2][oMetall] += kg;
					format(string, sizeof(string), "~r~-%d kg", kg);
					GameTextForPlayer(playerid, string, 2000, 1);
					format(string, sizeof(string), "%s %s[%d] {6699cc}положил(а) на склад %d кг металла", RankName(playerid),PlayerInfo[playerid][pName],playerid,kg);
					SendUnitMessage(playerid,0x00cc00AA,string);
					UpdateStoreMetall(1);
				}
				new caridasr = GetPlayerVehicleID(playerid);
				if(caridasr == svc[0])
				{
					if(metallcarMO[0] < kg) return SendClientMessage(playerid,COLOR_GRAD1, "В машине нет столько металла.");
					metallcarMO[0] -= kg;

					SendUnitMessage(playerid,0x00cc00AA,string);
					UpdateStoreMetall(1);
				}

				{

		    if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pMember] >= 6 && PlayerInfo[playerid][pMember] <= 9 || PlayerInfo[playerid][pMember] == 0 || PlayerInfo[playerid][pMember] == 13)
		    {
				if(GetPVarInt(playerid,"DrugsEffect") == 1) return SendClientMessage(playerid,COLOR_GRAD1, "Нельзя употреблять наркотики слишком часто...");
				new gramm;
				tmp = strtok(cmdtext, idx);
				gramm = strval(tmp);
				if(!strlen(tmp)) return SendClientMessage(playerid, COLOR_GRAD1, "Используйте: /drugs [грамм]");
				if(gramm <= 0) return SendClientMessage(playerid,COLOR_GRAD1, "Неверное кол-во грамм.");
				if(gramm > 20) return SendClientMessage(playerid,COLOR_GRAD1, "Не более 10 грамм за раз.");
				if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pDrugs] < gramm) return SendClientMessage(playerid,COLOR_GRAD1, "У Вас нет столько грамм наркотиков.");
				if(gramm >= 1 && gramm <= 3)
				{
					if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pHealth] < 100.0) PlayerInfo[playerid][pHealth] += 5.0;
					if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pHealth] > 100.0) PlayerInfo[playerid][pHealth] = 100.0;
					SetTimerEx("DrugsEffect", 6000, false, "i", playerid);
					SetPlayerDrunkLevel(playerid, 3000);
				}
				if(gramm >= 4 && gramm <= 6)
				{
					if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pHealth] < 100.0) PlayerInfo[playerid][pHealth] += 20.0;
					if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pHealth] > 100.0) PlayerInfo[playerid][pHealth] = 100.0;
					SetTimerEx("DrugsEffect", 12000, false, "i", playerid);
					SetPlayerDrunkLevel(playerid, 6000);
				}
				if(gramm >= 7 && gramm <= 10)
				{
					if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pHealth] < 100.0) PlayerInfo[playerid][pHealth] += 35.0;
					if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pHealth] > 100.0) PlayerInfo[playerid][pHealth] = 100.0;
					SetTimerEx("DrugsEffect", 20000, false, "i", playerid);
					SetPlayerDrunkLevel(playerid, 9000);
				}

					if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pHealth] < 100.0) PlayerInfo[playerid][pHealth] += 50.0;

					SetTimerEx("DrugsEffect", 30000, false, "i", playerid);
					SetPlayerDrunkLevel(playerid, 15000);
				}

					if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pHealth] < 100.0) PlayerInfo[playerid][pHealth] += 70.0;
					if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pHealth] > 100.0) PlayerInfo[playerid][pHealth] = 100.0;
					SetTimerEx("DrugsEffect", 50000, false, "i", playerid);
					SetPlayerDrunkLevel(playerid, 30000);
				}
				PlayerInfo[playerid][pDrugs] -= gramm;
				if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pSex] == 1) format(string, sizeof(string), "{DD90FF}%s употребил(а) {FF9915}%d г {DD90FF}наркотиков", PlayerInfo[playerid][pName],gramm);

	if(strcmp(cmd, "/lock", true) == 0)
	{
		if(login_check[playerid] == true)

			new idcars;
			tmp = strtok(cmdtext, idx);
			idcars = strval(tmp);
			new Float:vehx, Float:vehy, Float:vehz;
			if(!strlen(tmp)) return SendClientMessage(playerid, COLOR_GRAD1, "Используйте: /lock [тип транспорта (1- Домашний транспорт , 2- Арендованный транспорт , 3- Рабочий транспорт , 4- Доверенный транспорт)]");
			if(idcars == 1)
			{
				if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pHouse] < 999)
				{
					if(HouseInfo[PlayerInfo[playerid][pHouse]][hCar] == 0) return SendClientMessage(playerid, COLOR_GRAD, "У Вас нет домашнего транспорта!");
					GetVehiclePos(caridhouse[playerid], vehx, vehy, vehz);
					if(!IsPlayerInRangeOfPoint(playerid,15.0,vehx,vehy,vehz)) return SendClientMessage(playerid, COLOR_GRAD, "Вы должны находиться рядом с машиной.");
					GetVehicleParamsEx(caridhouse[playerid],VehInfo[caridhouse[playerid]][pEngine],VehInfo[caridhouse[playerid]][pLights],VehInfo[caridhouse[playerid]][pAlarm],VehInfo[caridhouse[playerid]][pDoors],VehInfo[caridhouse[playerid]][pBonnet],VehInfo[caridhouse[playerid]][pBoot],VehInfo[caridhouse[playerid]][pObjective]);
					if(VehInfo[caridhouse[playerid]][pDoors] == 1)
					{
						VehInfo[caridhouse[playerid]][pDoors] = 0;
						SetVehicleParamsEx(caridhouse[playerid],VehInfo[caridhouse[playerid]][pEngine],VehInfo[caridhouse[playerid]][pLights],VehInfo[caridhouse[playerid]][pAlarm],0,VehInfo[caridhouse[playerid]][pBonnet],VehInfo[caridhouse[playerid]][pBoot],VehInfo[caridhouse[playerid]][pObjective]);
						GameTextForPlayer(playerid, "~g~Open", 1000, 4);
						SetPlayerChatBubble(playerid,"открыл(а) автомобиль",COLOR_PURPLE,30.0,10000);
						PlayerPlaySound(playerid, 25800, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
					}
					else
					{
						VehInfo[caridhouse[playerid]][pDoors] = 1;
						SetVehicleParamsEx(caridhouse[playerid],VehInfo[caridhouse[playerid]][pEngine],VehInfo[caridhouse[playerid]][pLights],VehInfo[caridhouse[playerid]][pAlarm],1,VehInfo[caridhouse[playerid]][pBonnet],VehInfo[caridhouse[playerid]][pBoot],VehInfo[caridhouse[playerid]][pObjective]);
						GameTextForPlayer(playerid, "~r~Close", 1000, 4);
						SetPlayerChatBubble(playerid,"закрыл(а) автомобиль",COLOR_PURPLE,30.0,10000);
						PlayerPlaySound(playerid, 25800, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
					}
				}
			}
			if(idcars == 2)

				}

					GameTextForPlayer(playerid, "~r~Close", 1000, 4);
					SetPlayerChatBubble(playerid,"закрыл(а) автомобиль",COLOR_PURPLE,30.0,10000);
					PlayerPlaySound(playerid, 25800, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
				}
			}
			if(idcars == 4)
			{
				if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pAllowCar] == 0) return SendClientMessage(playerid, COLOR_GRAD, "У Вас нет доверенного транспорта!");
				GetVehiclePos(PlayerInfo[playerid][pAllowCar], vehx, vehy, vehz);
				if(!IsPlayerInRangeOfPoint(playerid,15.0,vehx,vehy,vehz)) return SendClientMessage(playerid, COLOR_GRAD, "Вы должны находиться рядом с машиной.");
				GetVehicleParamsEx(PlayerInfo[playerid][pAllowCar],VehInfo[PlayerInfo[playerid][pAllowCar]][pEngine],VehInfo[PlayerInfo[playerid][pAllowCar]][pLights],VehInfo[PlayerInfo[playerid][pAllowCar]][pAlarm],VehInfo[PlayerInfo[playerid][pAllowCar]][pDoors],VehInfo[PlayerInfo[playerid][pAllowCar]][pBonnet],VehInfo[PlayerInfo[playerid][pAllowCar]][pBoot],VehInfo[PlayerInfo[playerid][pAllowCar]][pObjective]);
				if(VehInfo[PlayerInfo[playerid][pAllowCar]][pDoors] == 1)
				{
					VehInfo[PlayerInfo[playerid][pAllowCar]][pDoors] = 0;
					SetVehicleParamsEx(PlayerInfo[playerid][pAllowCar],VehInfo[PlayerInfo[playerid][pAllowCar]][pEngine],VehInfo[PlayerInfo[playerid][pAllowCar]][pLights],VehInfo[PlayerInfo[playerid][pAllowCar]][pAlarm],0,VehInfo[PlayerInfo[playerid][pAllowCar]][pBonnet],VehInfo[PlayerInfo[playerid][pAllowCar]][pBoot],VehInfo[PlayerInfo[playerid][pAllowCar]][pObjective]);
					GameTextForPlayer(playerid, "~g~Open", 1000, 4);
					SetPlayerChatBubble(playerid,"открыл(а) автомобиль",COLOR_PURPLE,30.0,10000);
					PlayerPlaySound(playerid, 25800, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
				}
				else
				{
					VehInfo[PlayerInfo[playerid][pAllowCar]][pDoors] = 1;
					SetVehicleParamsEx(PlayerInfo[playerid][pAllowCar],VehInfo[PlayerInfo[playerid][pAllowCar]][pEngine],VehInfo[PlayerInfo[playerid][pAllowCar]][pLights],VehInfo[PlayerInfo[playerid][pAllowCar]][pAlarm],1,VehInfo[PlayerInfo[playerid][pAllowCar]][pBonnet],VehInfo[PlayerInfo[playerid][pAllowCar]][pBoot],VehInfo[PlayerInfo[playerid][pAllowCar]][pObjective]);

			}
		}

	{

		new givesmsid;
		tmp = strtok(cmdtext, idx);
		nphone = strval(tmp);
		if(!strlen(tmp)) return SendClientMessage(playerid, COLOR_GRAD1, "Используйте: /sms [номер телефона] [текст]");
		if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pPhone] >= 1 && login_check[playerid] == true)
		{
			if(PlayerInfo[playerid][pMuted] == 1) return SendClientMessage(playerid, 0xff6600AA, "Доступ в чат заблокирован. Узнать время до окончания бана чата {66cc33}/time");

			if(nphone == 0) return SendClientMessage(playerid, COLOR_GRAD, "Номер телефона введён неверно.");
			givesmsid = -1;
			foreach(new z : Player)
			{
				if(login_check[playerid] == true)
				{
					if(PlayerInfo[z][pPhone] == nphone) givesmsid = z;
				}
			}
			if(givesmsid == -1) return SendClientMessage(playerid, COLOR_GRAD, "Абонент вне зоны действия сети.");
			if(PlayerInfo[givesmsid][pTPhone] == false) return SendClientMessage(playerid, COLOR_GRAD, "Абонент вне зоны действия сети.");
			new length = strlen(cmdtext);
			while ((idx < length) && (cmdtext[idx] <= ' '))
			{
				idx++;
			}
			new offset = idx;
			new result[64];
			while ((idx < length) && ((idx - offset) < (sizeof(result) - 1)))
			{
				result[idx - offset] = cmdtext[idx];
				idx++;
			}
			result[idx - offset] = EOS;
			if(!strlen(result)) return SendClientMessage(playerid, COLOR_GRAD1, "Используйте: /sms [номер телефона] [текст]");
			if(strlen(result) > 64) return SendClientMessage(playerid,COLOR_GRAD1, "Слишком длинное сообщение.");
			GameTextForPlayer(playerid, "~r~-5$~n~~b~SMS", 2000, 1);
			PlayerInfo[playerid][pPhoneMoney] -= 5;
			format(query, sizeof(query), "SMS: %s | Отправитель: %s [т. %d]", (result),PlayerInfo[playerid][pName],PlayerInfo[playerid][pPhone]);
			SendClientMessage(givesmsid, COLOR_YELLOW , query);
			PlayerPlaySound(playerid, 21001, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
			format(query, sizeof(query), "SMS: %s | Получатель: %s [т. %d]", (result),PlayerInfo[givesmsid][pName],nphone);
			SendClientMessage(playerid, COLOR_YELLOW , query);
			SetPlayerChatBubble(playerid, "SMS >>>", COLOR_YELLOW, 15.0, 2000);
			SetPlayerChatBubble(givesmsid, "SMS <<<", COLOR_YELLOW, 15.0, 2000);
			if(adm_sms == true)
			{
				new strina[200];
				format(strina, sizeof(strina), "[A][SMS] %s | Отправил %s[%d] для %s[%d]", (result),PlayerInfo[playerid][pName],playerid,PlayerInfo[givesmsid][pName],givesmsid);

			}
		}
		else

		}
